<br>
A sign in attempt requires further verification because we did not recognize your device. To complete the sign in, enter the verification code on the unrecognized device.<br>
<br>
Device: Chrome on Windows<br>
Verification code: 351107<br>
<br>
If you did not attempt to sign in to your account, your password may be compromised. Visit <a href="https://github.com/settings/security" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://github.com/settings/security&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1715368548323000&amp;usg=AOvVaw1cjjz2EdulxFxKE0aBEIBn">https://github.com/settings/se<wbr>curity</a> to create a new, strong password for your GitHub account.<br>
<br>
If you'd like to automatically verify devices in the future, consider enabling two-factor authentication on your account. Visit <a href="https://docs.github.com/articles/configuring-two-factor-authentication" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.github.com/articles/configuring-two-factor-authentication&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1715368548323000&amp;usg=AOvVaw3QPhu_EDOKnlVNAXBJZb6B">https://docs.github.com/articl<wbr>es/configuring-two-factor-<wbr>authentication</a> to learn about two-factor authentication.<br>
<br>
If you decide to enable two-factor authentication, ensure you retain access to one or more account recovery methods. See <a href="https://docs.github.com/articles/configuring-two-factor-authentication-recovery-methods" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" data-saferedirecturl="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://docs.github.com/articles/configuring-two-factor-authentication-recovery-methods&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1715368548323000&amp;usg=AOvVaw3jZpnW9H-VMmrvsqMK_kTC">https://docs.github.com/articl<wbr>es/configuring-two-factor-<wbr>authentication-recovery-<wbr>methods</a> in the GitHub Help.<br>
